	</label>

	</div>

<div class="MainPage__row MainPage__header">
<div class="MainPage__block MainPage__intro">
<div class="mw-heading mw-heading1"><h1 id="Meta-Wiki" data-mw-thread-id="h-Meta-Wiki"><span data-mw-comment-start="" id="h-Meta-Wiki"></span>Meta-Wiki<span data-mw-comment-end="h-Meta-Wiki"></span></h1></div>
<div id="mf-intro" class="MainPage__block_contents">
<p><b>Welcome to <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Meta:About" title="Special:MyLanguage/Meta:About">Meta-Wiki</a></b>, the global community site for the <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Foundation" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation's</a> <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_projects" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia projects">projects</a> and related projects, from coordination and documentation to planning and analysis.
</p><p>Other meta-focused wikis such as <a href="https://outreach.wikimedia.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="outreach:">Wikimedia Outreach</a> are specialized projects that have their roots in Meta-Wiki. Related discussions also take place on Wikimedia <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Mailing_lists/Overview" title="Special:MyLanguage/Mailing lists/Overview">mailing lists</a> (particularly <b><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Mailing_lists#Wikimedia_mailing_list" title="Special:MyLanguage/Mailing lists">wikimedia-l</a></b>, with its low-traffic equivalent <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Mailing_lists#Wikimedia_Announcements_mailing_list" title="Special:MyLanguage/Mailing lists">WikimediaAnnounce</a>), <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/IRC" title="Special:MyLanguage/IRC">IRC channels</a> on Libera, individual wikis of <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_movement_affiliates" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia movement affiliates">Wikimedia affiliates</a>, and other places.
</p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="MainPage__block MainPage__menu">
<div class="MainPage__block_contents">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Mission" title="Special:MyLanguage/Mission">Mission</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_projects" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia projects">Projects</a><br /> (<a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Complete_list_of_Wikimedia_projects" title="Special:MyLanguage/Complete list of Wikimedia projects">complete list</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Research:Index" title="Special:MyLanguage/Research:Index">Research</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Meta:Babylon" title="Special:MyLanguage/Meta:Babylon">Translation</a><br /> (<a href="/wiki/Translation_requests" class="mw-redirect" title="Translation requests">requests</a>)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Vision" title="Special:MyLanguage/Vision">Vision</a></li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>

<div class="MainPage__block_heading"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg/20px-Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg/40px-Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg.png 1.5x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="900" /></span></span> Community and communication
</div>
<div class="MainPage__block_contents">
<div class="floatright"><bdi lang="en" dir="ltr" class="plainlinks" style="font-size:smaller;"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Translate/page-Template:Main_Page/Community_and_communication&amp;language=en&amp;action=page">+/−</a></bdi></div>
<div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Meta:Babel" title="Special:MyLanguage/Meta:Babel">Babel</a>, a discussion place for Meta-Wiki matters</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Mailing_lists" title="Special:MyLanguage/Mailing lists">Mailing lists</a> and <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/IRC" title="Special:MyLanguage/IRC">IRC</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Newsletters" title="Special:MyLanguage/Newsletters">Newsletters</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Meetup" title="Special:MyLanguage/Meetup">Meetups</a>, a list of offline events</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Embassy" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Embassy">Wikimedia Embassy</a>, a list of local contacts by language</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Forum" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Forum">Wikimedia Forum</a>, a multilingual forum for Wikimedia projects</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedian" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedian">Wikimedians</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Resource_Center" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Resource Center">Wikimedia Resource Center</a>, a hub for Wikimedia Foundation resources</li></ul>
</div>

<div class="MainPage__block MainPage__sister_projects">
<div class="MainPage__block_heading"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg/20px-Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg.png" decoding="async" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg/40px-Wikimedia_Community_Logo_optimized.svg.png 1.5x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="900" /></span></span> Wikimedia Foundation, Meta-Wiki, and its sister projects
</div>
<div class="MainPage__block_contents">
<div class="floatright"><bdi lang="en" dir="ltr" class="plainlinks" style="font-size:smaller;"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Translate/page-Template:Main_Page/Wikimedia_Foundation&amp;language=en&amp;action=page">+/−</a></bdi></div><div><bdi lang="en">The <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_Foundation" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation</a> is the overarching non-profit foundation that owns the <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia_servers" title="Special:MyLanguage/Wikimedia servers">Wikimedia servers</a> along with the domain names, <a href="/wiki/Logo" title="Logo">logos</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wikimedia_trademarks" title="Wikimedia trademarks">trademarks</a> of all <a href="/wiki/Special:MyLanguage/Complete_list_of_Wikimedia_projects" title="Special:MyLanguage/Complete list of Wikimedia projects">Wikimedia projects</a> and <a href="https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/" class="extiw" title="mw:">MediaWiki</a>. Meta-Wiki is the coordination wiki for the various Wikimedia wikis.</bdi></div><div style="clear:both;"></div>
<div class="floatright"><bdi lang="en" dir="ltr" class="plainlinks" style="font-size:smaller;"><a class="external text" href="https://meta.wikimedia.org/w/index.php?title=Special:Translate/page-Template:Main_Page/Sisterprojects&amp;language=en&amp;action=page">+/−</a></bdi></div><div><div class="MainPageSisterProjects__wrapper plainlinks" lang="en" dir="ltr">
